<h3 class="font-h3 text-h3 text-on-surface mb-md">Description</h3>
<div class="prose max-w-none text-on-surface-variant font-body-md text-body-md leading-relaxed space-y-4">
<p>This session focuses on acceleration mechanics under load. Ensure the sled weight is exactly 25% of the athlete's body weight. The transition from push to unresisted sprint must be instantaneous to maximize post-activation performance enhancement.</p>
<ul class="list-disc pl-5 space-y-2">
<li>Warm-up protocol Alpha (15 mins)</li>
<li>Focus on low heel recovery during the initial 10m of the push</li>
<li>Maintain stiff ankles and high hip position</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Note:</strong> Record times using the automated timing gates. Ensure conditions are logged in the weather module.</p>

<script>
        const settingsBtn = document.getElementById('settings-btn');
        const closePanel = document.getElementById('close-panel');
        const saveLayout = document.getElementById('save-layout');
        const panel = document.getElementById('customization-panel');

        function togglePanel() {
            panel.classList.toggle('translate-x-full');
            if (!panel.classList.contains('translate-x-full')) {
                settingsBtn.classList.add('text-[#c8102e]', 'bg-red-50');
            } else {
                settingsBtn.classList.remove('text-[#c8102e]', 'bg-red-50');
            }
        }

        settingsBtn.addEventListener('click', togglePanel);
        closePanel.addEventListener('click', togglePanel);
        saveLayout.addEventListener('click', togglePanel);
    </script>
